Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

017474,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
017475,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
017476,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
017477,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
017478,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
017479,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
017480,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except

017482,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
017483,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.

017497,000027:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017498,000028:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017499,000029:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017500,000030:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017501,000031: 
017502,000032:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017503,000033: 
017504,000034:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017505,000035:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017506,000036:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017507,000037:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017508,000038:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017509,000039:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017510,000040:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017511,000041:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017512,000042:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017513,000043: 
017514,000044:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017515,000045:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017516,000046:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017517,000047:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017518,000048:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017519,000049:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017520,000050:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017555,000085: 
017556,000086:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017557,000087: 
017558,000088:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017559,000089:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017560,000090:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017561,000091:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017562,000092:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017563,000093: 
017564,000094:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017565,000095:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017566,000096:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017567,000097:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017568,000098: 
017569,000099:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017570,000100:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017571,000101:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017572,000102:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017573,000103:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017574,000104: 
017575,000105:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
017576,000106:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017577,000107:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017578,000108:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 404 

017580,000110:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017581,000111:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017582,000112:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017583,000113:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017584,000114:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017585,000115:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017586,000116:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017587,000117:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017588,000118:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017589,000119:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017590,000120: 
017591,000121:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017592,000122:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017593,000123:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017594,000124: 
017595,000125: 
017596,000126:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017597,000127: 
017598,000128:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017599,000129:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017600,000130:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017601,000131: 
017602,000132:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017603,000133:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017604,000134:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017605,000135:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017606,000136:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017607,000137:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017608,000138:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017609,000139: 
017610,000140:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017611,000141:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017612,000142: 
017613,000143: 
017614,000144:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017615,000145: 
017616,000146:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017617,000147:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017618,000148:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017619,000149:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017620,000150: 
017621,000151: 
017622,000152:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017623,000153: 
017624,000154:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017625,000155:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017626,000156:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017627,000157:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017628,000158: 
017629,000159:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 405 

017631,000161:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017632,000162: 
017633,000163: 
017634,000164:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017635,000165: 
017636,000166:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017637,000167:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017638,000168: 
017639,000169:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017640,000170:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017641,000171:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017642,000172:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017643,000173: 
017644,000174:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017645,000175:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017646,000176: 
017647,000177:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017648,000178:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017649,000179:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017650,000180:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017651,000181: 
017652,000182:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017653,000183:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017654,000184: 
017655,000185:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017656,000186:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017657,000187: 
017658,000188:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017659,000189: 
017660,000190:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017661,000191:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017662,000192:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017663,000193:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017664,000194: 
017665,000195:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017666,000196:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017667,000197: 
017668,000198:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017669,000199:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017670,000200: 
017671,000201: 
017672,000202:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017673,000203:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017674,000204:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017675,000205:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017697,000227:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017698,000228: 
017699,000229:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017700,000230:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017701,000231:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017702,000232:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017703,000233:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017704,000234:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017705,000235:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017706,000236:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017707,000237:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017708,000238:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017709,000239:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017710,000240:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017711,000241:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017712,000242:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017713,000243:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017714,000244:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017715,000245:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017716,000246:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017717,000247:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017718,000248:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017719,000249:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017720,000250:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017721,000251:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE+1
017722,000252:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017723,000253:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER,11-13,C RELAYS
017724,000254:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017725,000255:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017726,000256:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017727,000257:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017728,000258:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017729,000259:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017730,000260:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017731,000261:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017732,000262:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017733,000263:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017734,000264:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

017841,000371:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
017842,000372:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
017843,000373:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
017844,000374:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
017845,000375:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
017846,000376:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
017847,000377:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
017848,000378:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
017849,000379:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
017850,000380:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
017851,000381:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
017852,000382:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017854,000384: 
017855,000385: 
017856,000386:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017857,000387:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017858,000388:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017859,000389:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017860,000390:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017861,000391:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017862,000392: 
017863,000393:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017864,000394:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017865,000395:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017866,000396:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017867,000397:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017868,000398:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017869,000399: 
017870,000400:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017871,000401:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
017872,000402:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
017873,000403:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
017874,000404:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
017875,000405:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
017876,000406:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
017877,000407:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
017878,000408:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
017879,000409:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
017880,000410:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
017881,000411:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017882,000412: 
017883,000413: 
017884,000414:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017885,000415: 
017886,000416:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017887,000417:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017888,000418:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017889,000419:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017890,000420:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017891,000421:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 410 

017893,000423:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017894,000424:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017895,000425:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017896,000426:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017897,000427:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017898,000428:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017899,000429:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017900,000430:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017901,000431: 
017902,000432: 
017903,000433:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017904,000434:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
017905,000435:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
017906,000436:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
017907,000437:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
017908,000438:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
017909,000439:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
017910,000440:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
017911,000441:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
017912,000442:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
017913,000443:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
017914,000444:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
017915,000445: 
017916,000446: 
017917,000447:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
017918,000448: 
017919,000449:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
017920,000450:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
017921,000451:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
017922,000452:

018630,001160:

Page 426 

018632,001162:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018633,001163:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018634,001164:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018635,001165:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018636,001166:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018637,001167:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018638,001168: 
018639,001169:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018640,001170:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018641,001171: 
018642,001172:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018643,001173: 
018644,001174:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018645,001175:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018646,001176:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018647,001177: 
018648,001178:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018649,001179:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018650,001180:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018651,001181:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018652,001182:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018653,001183:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018654,001184: 
018655,001185:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018656,001186:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018657,001187:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018658,001188:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018659,001189:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018660,001190: 
018661,001191:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018662,001192:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018663,001193:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018664,001194:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018665,001195:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018666,001196:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018667,001197:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018668,001198:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018669,001199: 
018670,001200: 
018671,001201:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018672,001202:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018673,001203:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018674,001204: 
018675,001205: 
018676,001206:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018677,001207:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018678,001208: 
018679,001209:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018680,001210:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018681,001211:

Page 427 

018683,001213:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018684,001214: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018685,001215: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018686,001216: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
018687,001217: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
018688,001218: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2                         
018689,001219: 41,2360           44753        DSPAB              CS       ONE                                   
018690,001220: 41,2361           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018691,001221: 41,2362           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD

019828,002358:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019829,002359:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019830,002360:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019831,002361:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019832,002362:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019833,002363: 
019834,002364:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019835,002365:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019836,002366:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019837,002367:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019838,002368:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019839,002369:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019840,002370:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019841,002371: 
019842,002372:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019843,002373:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019844,002374:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019845,002375: 
019846,002376:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019847,002377:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019848,002378: 
019849,002379:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019850,002380:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019851,002381: 
019852,002382:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

019979,002509:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
019980,002510:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
019981,002511:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
019982,002512: 
019983,002513:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
019984,002514: 
019985,002515:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
019986,002516:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
019987,002517:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
019988,002518: 
019989,002519:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
019990,002520:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
019991,002521:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
019992,002522: 
019993,002523: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
019994,002524: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
019995,002525: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
019996,002526: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
019997,002527: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
019998,002528: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
019999,002529: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWO                              
020000,002530: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

Page 463 

020430,002960:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020431,002961: 
020432,002962:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020433,002963: 
020434,002964:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020435,002965:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020436,002966:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020437,002967:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020438,002968: 
020439,002969:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020440,002970:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020441,002971:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020442,002972: 
020443,002973:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020444,002974:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020445,002975:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020446,002976:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020447,002977:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020448,002978:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020449,002979:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020450,002980:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020451,002981:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020452,002982:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020453,002983:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020454,002984: 
020455,002985: 40,3457           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020456,002986: 40,3460           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020457,002987: 40,3461           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
020458,002988: 40,3462           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020459,002989: 40,3463           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020460,002990: 40,3464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020461,002991: 40,3465           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020462,002992: 40,3466           03475                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020463,002993: 40,3467           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020464,002994: 40,3470           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020465,002995: 40,3471           03473                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020466,002996: 40,3472           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020467,002997: 40,3473           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020468,002998: 40,3474           20723                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020469,002999: 40,3475           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020470,003000: 40,3476           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020471,003001: 40,3477           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020472,003002: 40,3500           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020473,003003: 40,3501           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020474,003004: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020475,003005: 
020476,003006: 40,3503                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020477,003007:

Page 464 

020479,003009:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020480,003010:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020481,003011:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020482,003012:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020483,003013:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020484,003014: 
020485,003015:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020486,003016:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020487,003017:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020488,003018: 
020489,003019:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020490,003020:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020491,003021: 
020492,003022:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020493,003023:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020494,003024:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020495,003025:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020496,003026:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020497,003027: 
020498,003028:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020499,003029:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020500,003030:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020501,003031:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020502,003032: 
020503,003033:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020504,003034:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020505,003035:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020506,003036:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020507,003037:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020508,003038:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020509,003039:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020510,003040: 
020511,003041:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020512,003042:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020513,003043: 
020514,003044:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020515,003045:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020516,003046: 
020517,003047:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020518,003048:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020519,003049: 
020520,003050:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020521,003051:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020522,003052:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020523,003053:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020524,003054:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020525,003055:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020526,003056:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020527,003057: 
020528,003058:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 465 

020530,003060:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020531,003061:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020532,003062:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020533,003063:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020534,003064:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020535,003065:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020536,003066:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020537,003067:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020538,003068:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020539,003069: 
020540,003070:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020541,003071:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020542,003072: 
020543,003073:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
020544,003074: 
020545,003075:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020654,003184:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020655,003185:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020656,003186:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020657,003187:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020658,003188:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020659,003189:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020660,003190: 
020661,003191: 
020662,003192:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020663,003193:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020664,003194:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020665,003195:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020666,003196:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020667,003197: 
020668,003198: 
020669,003199:                                                                                                  #  L  TO ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020670,003200:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020671,003201:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020672,003202:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020673,003203:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020674,003204:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020675,003205:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020676,003206:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020677,003207:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020678,003208:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020679,003209: 
020680,003210: 
020681,003211:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 468 

020683,003213:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020684,003214:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020685,003215:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020686,003216:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020687,003217:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020688,003218: 
020689,003219:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020690,003220:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020691,003221:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020692,003222:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020693,003223:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020694,003224:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020695,003225:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020696,003226:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020697,003227: 
020698,003228: 
020699,003229:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020700,003230: 
020701,003231: 
020702,003232:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020703,003233:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

020812,003342:                                                                                                  #  DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY MODREG DIRECTLY. IT PUTS IN EXEC REQUEST WITH
020813,003343:                                                                                                  #  PRIO 30000 FOR DSPMMJB AND RETURNS TO CALLER.

020816,003346: 
020817,003347:                                                                                                  #  DSPMM MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT CAN BE CALLED VIA BANKCALL.
