Page 476 

021044,003574:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021045,003575: 
021046,003576:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021047,003577:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021048,003578:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021049,003579:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021050,003580: 
021051,003581:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021052,003582:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021053,003583:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021054,003584:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021055,003585:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021056,003586:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021057,003587:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021058,003588: 
021059,003589: 
021060,003590:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021061,003591:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021062,003592:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021063,003593:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021064,003594:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021065,003595: 
021066,003596: 
021067,003597:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021068,003598:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021069,003599:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021070,003600:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021071,003601:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021072,003602: 
021073,003603: 
021074,003604:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021075,003605:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021076,003606:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021077,003607: 
021078,003608: 
021079,003609:                                                                                                  #  .
021080,003610: 
021081,003611: 
021082,003612:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021083,003613:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021084,003614:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
021085,003615:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021086,003616: 
021087,003617: 
021088,003618:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021089,003619:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021090,003620:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021091,003621:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021092,003622:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021093,003623:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

021095,003625:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021096,003626: 
021097,003627:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
021098,003628:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
021099,003629:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
021100,003630:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021101,003631:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021102,003632:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021103,003633: 
021104,003634:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021105,003635:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021106,003636: 
021107,003637: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021108,003638: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021109,003639: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021110,003640: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021111,003641: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021112,003642: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021113,003643: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021114,003644: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021115,003645: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021116,003646: 
021117,003647: 
021118,003648:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021119,003649:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021120,003650:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021121,003651:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021122,003652:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021123,003653: 
021124,003654:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021125,003655:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021126,003656:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021127,003657:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021128,003658:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021129,003659:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021130,003660:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021131,003661:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021132,003662:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021133,003663:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021134,003664:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021135,003665:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021136,003666:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021137,003667: 
021138,003668: 
021139,003669:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
021140,003670:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
021141,003671:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
021142,003672:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
021143,003673:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
021144,003674:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

021290,003820:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
021291,003821:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021292,003822:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021293,003823:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021294,003824:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021295,003825:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
021296,003826:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
